## Device state parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Configures device inactivity detection, state persistence strategy, and rate limits for state rule nodes.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">DEFAULT&#95;INACTIVITY&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>600</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Device inactivity timeout is a global configuration parameter that defines when the device will be marked as "inactive" by the server.  The parameter value is in seconds. A user can overwrite this parameter for an individual device by setting the “inactivityTimeout” server-side attribute (NOTE: expects value in milliseconds).  We recommend this parameter to be in sync with session inactivity timeout ("transport.sessions.inactivity&#95;timeout" or TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;SESSIONS&#95;INACTIVITY&#95;TIMEOUT) parameter  which is responsible for detection of the stale device connection sessions.  The value of the session inactivity timeout parameter should be greater or equal to the device inactivity timeout.  Note that the session inactivity timeout is set in milliseconds while device inactivity timeout is in seconds.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">DEFAULT&#95;STATE&#95;CHECK&#95;INTERVAL</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval for checking the device state after a specified period. Time in seconds</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">PERSIST&#95;STATE&#95;TO&#95;TELEMETRY</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Controls whether we store the device 'active' flag in attributes (default) or telemetry.  If you decide to change this parameter, you should re-create the device info view as one of the following:  If 'persistToTelemetry' is changed from 'false' to 'true': 'CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW device&#95;info&#95;view AS SELECT &#42; FROM device&#95;info&#95;active&#95;ts&#95;view;'  If 'persistToTelemetry' is changed from 'true' to 'false': 'CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW device&#95;info&#95;view AS SELECT &#42; FROM device&#95;info&#95;active&#95;attribute&#95;view;'</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">STATE&#95;TELEMETRY&#95;TTL</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Millisecond value defining time-to-live for device state telemetry data (e.g. 'active', 'lastActivityTime').  Used only when state.persistToTelemetry is set to 'true' and Cassandra is used for timeseries data.  0 means time-to-live mechanism is disabled.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;DEVICE&#95;STATE&#95;INIT&#95;FETCH&#95;PACK&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>50000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Number of device records to fetch per batch when initializing device activity states</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">DEVICE&#95;STATE&#95;NODE&#95;RATE&#95;LIMIT&#95;CONFIGURATION</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1:1,30:60,60:3600</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Defines the rate at which device connectivity events can be triggered.  Comma-separated list of capacity:duration pairs that define bandwidth capacity and refill duration for token bucket rate limit algorithm.  Refill is set to be greedy. Please refer to Bucket4j library documentation for more details.</p>
  </div>
</div>

## TBEL parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Configures the ThingsBoard Expression Language (TBEL) engine: limits, timeouts, thread pool, and blacklisting.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable TBEL feature.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;MAX&#95;TOTAL&#95;ARGS&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>100000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Limit the number of arguments that are passed to the function to execute the script</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;MAX&#95;RESULT&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>300000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed symbols in a result after processing a script</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;MAX&#95;SCRIPT&#95;BODY&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>50000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed symbols in the script body</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;MAX&#95;MEMORY&#95;LIMIT&#95;MB</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>8</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed TBEL script execution memory</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;MAX&#95;ERRORS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>3</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed TBEL script execution errors before it will be blacklisted</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;MAX&#95;REQUEST&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>500</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">TBEL Eval max request timeout in milliseconds. 0 - no timeout</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;MAX&#95;BLACKLIST&#95;DURATION&#95;SEC</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum time in seconds for black listed function to stay in the list.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;THREAD&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>50</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specify thread pool size for javascript executor service</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TBEL&#95;COMPILED&#95;SCRIPTS&#95;CACHE&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum cache size of TBEL compiled scripts</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TBEL&#95;STATS&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable stats collection for TBEL engine</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TBEL&#95;STATS&#95;PRINT&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval of logging for TBEL stats</p>
  </div>
</div>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">

  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">JS&#95;MAX&#95;TOTAL&#95;ARGS&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>100000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Limit the number of arguments that are passed to the function to execute the script</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">JS&#95;MAX&#95;RESULT&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>300000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed symbols in a result after processing a script</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">JS&#95;MAX&#95;SCRIPT&#95;BODY&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>50000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed symbols in script body</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;THREAD&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>50</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specify thread pool size for javascript executor service</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">USE&#95;LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Use Sandboxed (secured) JVM JavaScript environment</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX&#95;MONITOR&#95;THREAD&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>4</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specify thread pool size for JavaScript sandbox resource monitor</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX&#95;MAX&#95;CPU&#95;TIME</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>8000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum CPU time in milliseconds allowed for script execution</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX&#95;MAX&#95;MEMORY</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>104857600</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum memory in Bytes which JS executor thread can allocate (approximate calculation). A zero memory limit in combination with a non-zero CPU limit is not recommended due to the implementation of Nashorn 0.4.2. 100MiB is effectively unlimited for most cases</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX&#95;MAX&#95;ERRORS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>3</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed JavaScript execution errors before JavaScript will be blacklisted</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;MAX&#95;REQUEST&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">JS Eval max request timeout. 0 - no timeout</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LOCAL&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX&#95;MAX&#95;BLACKLIST&#95;DURATION&#95;SEC</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum time in seconds for black listed function to stay in the list.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;JS&#95;LOCAL&#95;STATS&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable stats collection for local JS executor</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;JS&#95;LOCAL&#95;STATS&#95;PRINT&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval of logging for local JS executor stats</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">REMOTE&#95;JS&#95;THREAD&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>50</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specify thread pool size for javascript executor service</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">REMOTE&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX&#95;MAX&#95;ERRORS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>3</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed JavaScript execution errors before JavaScript will be blacklisted</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">REMOTE&#95;JS&#95;SANDBOX&#95;MAX&#95;BLACKLIST&#95;DURATION&#95;SEC</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum time in seconds for black listed function to stay in the list.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;JS&#95;REMOTE&#95;STATS&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable stats collection for remote JS executor</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;JS&#95;REMOTE&#95;STATS&#95;PRINT&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval of logging for remote JS executor stats</p>
  </div>
</div>

## Transport configuration parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Configures session management, rate limits, and protocol-specific settings for HTTP, MQTT, CoAP, LwM2M, and SNMP transports.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;SESSIONS&#95;INACTIVITY&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>600000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Session inactivity timeout is a global configuration parameter that defines how long the device transport session will be opened after the last message arrives from the device.  The parameter value is in milliseconds.  The last activity time of the device session is updated if the device sends any message, including keepalive messages  If there is no activity, the session will be closed, and all subscriptions will be deleted.  We recommend this parameter to be in sync with device inactivity timeout ("state.defaultInactivityTimeoutInSec" or DEFAULT&#95;INACTIVITY&#95;TIMEOUT) parameter  which is responsible for detection of the device connectivity status in the core service of the platform.  The value of the session inactivity timeout parameter should be greater or equal to the device inactivity timeout.  Note that the session inactivity timeout is set in milliseconds while device inactivity timeout is in seconds.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;SESSIONS&#95;REPORT&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>3000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval of periodic check for expired sessions and report of the changes to session last activity time</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;ACTIVITY&#95;REPORTING&#95;STRATEGY</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>LAST</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">This property specifies the strategy for reporting activity events within each reporting period.  The accepted values are 'FIRST', 'LAST', 'FIRST&#95;AND&#95;LAST' and 'ALL'.  <ul><li> 'FIRST': Only the first activity event in each reporting period is reported.</li>  <li> 'LAST': Only the last activity event in the reporting period is reported.</li>  <li> 'FIRST&#95;AND&#95;LAST': Both the first and last activity events in the reporting period are reported.</li>  <li> 'ALL': All activity events in the reporting period are reported.</li></ul></p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">JSON&#95;TYPE&#95;CAST&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Cast String data types to Numeric if possible when processing Telemetry/Attributes JSON</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">JSON&#95;MAX&#95;STRING&#95;VALUE&#95;LENGTH</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum allowed string value length when processing Telemetry/Attributes JSON (0 value disables string value length check)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">CLIENT&#95;SIDE&#95;RPC&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Processing timeout interval of the RPC command on the CLIENT SIDE. Time in milliseconds</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;API&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/disable http/mqtt/coap/lwm2m transport protocols (has higher priority than certain protocol's 'enabled' property)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;LOG&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable log of transport messages to telemetry. For example, logging of LwM2M registration update</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;LOG&#95;MAX&#95;LENGTH</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1024</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum length of the log message. The content will be truncated to the specified value if needed</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;IP&#95;RATE&#95;LIMITS&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable or disable generic rate limits. Device and Tenant-specific rate limits are controlled in Tenant Profile.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;MAX&#95;WRONG&#95;CREDENTIALS&#95;PER&#95;IP</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum number of connect attempts with invalid credentials</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;IP&#95;BLOCK&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Timeout (in milliseconds) to expire block IP addresses</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">HTTP&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable local HTTP transport protocol</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">HTTP&#95;REQUEST&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">HTTP request processing timeout in milliseconds</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">HTTP&#95;MAX&#95;REQUEST&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>300000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">HTTP maximum request processing timeout in milliseconds</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">HTTP&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;MAX&#95;PAYLOAD&#95;SIZE&#95;LIMIT&#95;CONFIGURATION</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>/api/v1/&#42;/rpc/&#42;&#42;=65536;/api/v1/&#42;&#42;=52428800</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Semi-colon-separated list of urlPattern=maxPayloadSize pairs that define max http request size for specified url pattern. After first match all other will be skipped</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/disable mqtt transport protocol.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;BIND&#95;ADDRESS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0.0.0.0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">MQTT bind-address</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;BIND&#95;PORT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1883</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">MQTT bind port</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;PROXY&#95;PROTOCOL&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable proxy protocol support. Disabled by default. If enabled, supports both v1 and v2.  Useful to get the real IP address of the client in the logs and for rate limits.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">MQTT processing timeout in milliseconds</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;DISCONNECT&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">MQTT disconnect timeout in milliseconds. The time to wait for the client to disconnect after the server sends a disconnect message.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;MSG&#95;QUEUE&#95;SIZE&#95;PER&#95;DEVICE&#95;LIMIT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>100</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">messages await in the queue before the device connected state. This limit works on the low level before TenantProfileLimits mechanism</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;GATEWAY&#95;METRICS&#95;REPORT&#95;INTERVAL&#95;SEC</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60</code></p>

  <div class="config-def-item">

    <p class="config-def-desc">Optional alias of the private key. If not set, the platform will load the first private key from the keystore</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">MQTT&#95;SSL&#95;KEY&#95;PASSWORD</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>server&#95;key&#95;password</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Optional password to access the private key. If not set, the platform will attempt to load the private keys that are not protected with the password;</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">

    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LWM2M&#95;DTLS&#95;CONNECTION&#95;ID&#95;LENGTH</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>8</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">LWM2M DTLS connection ID length for LWM2M. RFC 9146, Connection Identifier for DTLS 1.2  Default: off. <br />  Control usage of DTLS connection ID length (CID).  <ul> <li> 'off' to deactivate it. </li>  <li> 'on' to activate Connection ID support (same as CID 0 or more 0). </li>  <li> A positive value defines generated CID size in bytes.</li>  <li> A value of 0 means we accept using CID but will not generate one for foreign peer (enables support but not for incoming traffic). </li>  <li> A value between 0 and &lt;= 4: SingleNodeConnectionIdGenerator is used </li>  <li> A value that are &gt; 4: MultiNodeConnectionIdGenerator is used </li> </ul></p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">LWM2M&#95;SERVER&#95;ID</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>123</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">LwM2M Server ID</p>
  </div>

  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;TRANSPORT&#95;SSL&#95;CERTIFICATE&#95;RELOAD&#95;CHECK&#95;INTERVAL&#95;SECONDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval in seconds for certificate reload</p>
  </div>
</div>

## CoAP server parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Configures the standalone CoAP server bind address, port, DTLS encryption, and credential settings.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;SERVER&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/disable coap server.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;BIND&#95;ADDRESS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0.0.0.0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">CoAP bind address</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;BIND&#95;PORT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>5683</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">CoAP bind port</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/disable DTLS 1.2 support</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;RETRANSMISSION&#95;TIMEOUT&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>9000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">RFC7925&#95;RETRANSMISSION&#95;TIMEOUT&#95;IN&#95;MILLISECONDS = 9000</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;BIND&#95;ADDRESS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0.0.0.0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">CoAP DTLS bind address</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;BIND&#95;PORT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>5684</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">CoAP DTLS bind port</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;CONNECTION&#95;ID&#95;LENGTH</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>8</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">CoAP DTLS connection ID length. RFC 9146, Connection Identifier for DTLS 1.2  Default: off. <br />  Control usage of DTLS connection ID length (CID).  <ul> <li> 'off' to deactivate it. </li>  <li> 'on' to activate Connection ID support (same as CID 0 or more 0). </li>  <li> A positive value defines generated CID size in bytes.</li>  <li> A value of 0 means we accept using CID but will not generate one for foreign peer (enables support but not for incoming traffic).</li>  <li> A value between 0 and &lt;= 4: SingleNodeConnectionIdGenerator is used</li>  <li> A value that are &gt; 4: MultiNodeConnectionIdGenerator is used</li> </ul></p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;MAX&#95;TRANSMISSION&#95;UNIT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1024</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specify the MTU (Maximum Transmission Unit).  Should be used if LAN MTU is not used, e.g. if IP tunnels are used or if the client uses a smaller value than the LAN MTU.  Default = 1024  Minimum value = 64  If set to 0 - LAN MTU is used.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;MAX&#95;FRAGMENT&#95;LENGTH</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1024</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">DTLS maximum fragment length (RFC 6066, Section 4).  Default = 1024  Possible values: 512, 1024, 2048, 4096.  If set to 0, the default maximum fragment size of 2^14 bytes (16,384 bytes) is used.  Without this extension, TLS specifies a fixed maximum plaintext fragment length of 2^14 bytes.  It may be desirable for constrained clients to negotiate a smaller maximum fragment length due to memory limitations or bandwidth limitations.  In order to negotiate smaller maximum fragment lengths,  clients MAY include an extension of type "max&#95;fragment&#95;length" in the (extended) client hello.  The "extension&#95;data" field of this extension SHALL contain:  &lt;pre&gt; enum &#123;    2^9(1) == 512,    2^10(2) == 1024,    2^11(3) == 2048,    2^12(4) == 4096,    (255)  &#125; MaxFragmentLength; &lt;/pre&gt;  TLS already requires clients and servers to support fragmentation of handshake messages.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;CREDENTIALS&#95;TYPE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>PEM</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Server credentials type (PEM - pem certificate file; KEYSTORE - java keystore)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;PEM&#95;CERT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>coapserver.pem</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Path to the server certificate file (holds server certificate or certificate chain, may include server private key)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;PEM&#95;KEY</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>coapserver&#95;key.pem</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Path to the server certificate private key file. Optional by default. Required if the private key is not present in the server certificate file;</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;PEM&#95;KEY&#95;PASSWORD</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>server&#95;key&#95;password</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Server certificate private key password (optional)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;KEY&#95;STORE&#95;TYPE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>JKS</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Type of the key store (JKS or PKCS12)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;KEY&#95;STORE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>coapserver.jks</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Path to the key store that holds the SSL certificate</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;KEY&#95;STORE&#95;PASSWORD</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>server&#95;ks&#95;password</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Password used to access the key store</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;KEY&#95;ALIAS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>serveralias</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Key alias</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">COAP&#95;DTLS&#95;KEY&#95;PASSWORD</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>server&#95;key&#95;password</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Password used to access the key</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;COAP&#95;X509&#95;DTLS&#95;SKIP&#95;VALIDITY&#95;CHECK&#95;FOR&#95;CLIENT&#95;CERT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Skip certificate validity check for client certificates.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;COAP&#95;X509&#95;DTLS&#95;SESSION&#95;INACTIVITY&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>86400000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Inactivity timeout of DTLS session. Used to cleanup cache</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;COAP&#95;X509&#95;DTLS&#95;SESSION&#95;REPORT&#95;TIMEOUT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1800000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval of periodic eviction of the timed-out DTLS sessions</p>
  </div>
</div>

## Edges parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Controls Edge instance gRPC communication, event storage, state persistence, and statistics reporting.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/disable Edge instance</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;PORT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>7070</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">RPC port bind</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;CLIENT&#95;MAX&#95;KEEP&#95;ALIVE&#95;TIME&#95;SEC</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specifies the minimum amount of time that should elapse between keepalive pings sent by the client  This prevents clients from sending pings too frequently, which can be a nuisance to the server (potentially even a denial-of-service attack vector if abused)  If a client sends pings more frequently than this interval, the server may terminate the connection.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;KEEP&#95;ALIVE&#95;TIME&#95;SEC</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Sets the time of inactivity (no read operations on the connection) after which the server will send a keepalive ping to the client.  This is used to ensure that the connection is still alive and to prevent network intermediaries from dropping connections due to inactivity.  It's a way for the server to proactively check if the client is still responsive.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;KEEP&#95;ALIVE&#95;TIMEOUT&#95;SEC</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>5</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specifies the maximum amount of time the server waits for a response to its keepalive ping.  If the ping is not acknowledged within this time frame, the server considers the connection dead and may close it.  This timeout helps detect unresponsive clients.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;SSL&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/disable SSL support</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;SSL&#95;CERT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>certChainFile.pem</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Path to the server certificate file (holds server certificate or certificate chain, may include server private key).  Accepts an absolute filesystem path (e.g. /etc/thingsboard/certChainFile.pem),  a relative path resolved against the working directory first then the classpath,  or a classpath resource with the explicit "classpath:" prefix (e.g. classpath:conf/certChainFile.pem).</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;SSL&#95;PRIVATE&#95;KEY</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>privateKeyFile.pem</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Path to the server certificate private key file. Optional if the private key is already present in the cert file above.  Supports the same path resolution as 'cert': absolute, relative/classpath, or "classpath:" prefix.  Leave empty when using a combined PEM cert that already contains the private key.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;SSL&#95;KEY&#95;PASSWORD</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Server certificate private key password (optional). Leave empty if the key is not encrypted.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;MAX&#95;INBOUND&#95;MESSAGE&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>4194304</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum size (in bytes) of inbound messages the cloud can handle from the edge. By default, it can handle messages up to 4 Megabytes</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;RPC&#95;MAX&#95;TELEMETRY&#95;MESSAGE&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum length of telemetry (time-series and attributes) message the cloud sends to the edge. By default, there is no limitation.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;STORAGE&#95;MAX&#95;READ&#95;RECORDS&#95;COUNT</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>50</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Max records of edge event to read from DB and sent to the edge</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;NO&#95;READ&#95;RECORDS&#95;SLEEP</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Number of milliseconds to wait before the next check of edge events in DB</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;SLEEP&#95;BETWEEN&#95;BATCHES</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Number of milliseconds to wait before resending failed batch of edge events to edge</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;MISORDERING&#95;COMPENSATION&#95;MILLIS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Time (in milliseconds) to subtract from the start timestamp when fetching edge events.  This compensates for possible misordering between `created&#95;time` (used for partitioning)  and `seqId` (used for sorting). Without this, events with smaller seqId but larger created&#95;time  might be skipped, especially across partition boundaries.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;MAX&#95;HIGH&#95;PRIORITY&#95;QUEUE&#95;SIZE&#95;PER&#95;SESSION</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Max number of high priority edge events per edge session. No persistence - stored in memory</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;SCHEDULER&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>4</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Number of threads that are used to check DB for edge events</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;SEND&#95;SCHEDULER&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>4</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Number of threads that are used to send downlink messages to edge over gRPC</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;GRPC&#95;CALLBACK&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>4</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Number of threads that are used to convert edge events from DB into downlink messages and send them for delivery</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;PERSIST&#95;STATE&#95;TO&#95;TELEMETRY</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Persist state of edge (active, last connect, last disconnect) into timeseries or attributes tables. 'false' means to store edge state into attributes table</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;STATS&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>true</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable or disable reporting of edge communication stats (true or false)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;STATS&#95;TTL</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>30</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Time-to-live in days for stored edge communication stats in timeseries</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">EDGES&#95;STATS&#95;REPORT&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>600000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">How often to report edge communication stats in milliseconds</p>
  </div>
</div>

## Spring doc common parameters

  </div>

## Queue configuration parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Configures the message queue backend (in-memory or Kafka) and all topic/partition/consumer settings for each service.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;TYPE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>in-memory</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">in-memory or kafka (Apache Kafka)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;PREFIX</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Global queue prefix. If specified, prefix is added before default topic name: 'prefix.default&#95;topic&#95;name'. Prefix is applied to all topics (and consumer groups for kafka).</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;IN&#95;MEMORY&#95;STATS&#95;PRINT&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">For debug level</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;SERVERS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>localhost:9092</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Kafka Bootstrap nodes in "host:port" format</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;SSL&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable SSL Kafka communication</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;SSL&#95;TRUSTSTORE&#95;LOCATION</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The location of the trust store file</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;SSL&#95;TRUSTSTORE&#95;PASSWORD</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The password of trust store file if specified</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;SSL&#95;KEYSTORE&#95;LOCATION</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The location of the key store file. This is optional for the client and can be used for two-way authentication for the client</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;SSL&#95;KEYSTORE&#95;PASSWORD</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The store password for the key store file. This is optional for the client and only needed if ‘ssl.keystore.location’ is configured. Key store password is not supported for PEM format</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;SSL&#95;KEY&#95;PASSWORD</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The password of the private key in the key store file or the PEM key specified in ‘keystore.key’</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;ACKS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>all</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The number of acknowledgments the producer requires the leader to have received before considering a request complete. This controls the durability of records that are sent. The following settings are allowed:0, 1 and all</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;RETRIES</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Number of retries. Resend any record whose send fails with a potentially transient error</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;COMPRESSION&#95;TYPE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>none</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">none, gzip or lz4</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;BATCH&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>16384</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Default batch size. This setting gives the upper bound of the batch size to be sent</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;LINGER&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">This variable creates a small amount of artificial delay—that is, rather than immediately sending out a record</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;MAX&#95;REQUEST&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1048576</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The maximum size of a request in bytes. This setting will limit the number of record batches the producer will send in a single request to avoid sending huge requests</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;KAFKA&#95;MAX&#95;IN&#95;FLIGHT&#95;REQUESTS&#95;PER&#95;CONNECTION</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>5</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The maximum number of unacknowledged requests the client will send on a single connection before blocking</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;BUFFER&#95;MEMORY</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>33554432</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The total bytes of memory the producer can use to buffer records waiting to be sent to the server</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;REPLICATION&#95;FACTOR</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The multiple copies of data over the multiple brokers of Kafka</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>300000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The maximum delay between invocations of poll() method when using consumer group management. This places an upper bound on the amount of time that the consumer can be idle before fetching more records</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>8192</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The maximum number of records returned in a single call of poll() method</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;MAX&#95;PARTITION&#95;FETCH&#95;BYTES</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>16777216</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The maximum amount of data per-partition the server will return. Records are fetched in batches by the consumer</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;FETCH&#95;MAX&#95;BYTES</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>134217728</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The maximum amount of data the server will return. Records are fetched in batches by the consumer</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;REQUEST&#95;TIMEOUT&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>30000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">(30 seconds)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;SESSION&#95;TIMEOUT&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">(10 seconds)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;AUTO&#95;OFFSET&#95;RESET</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>earliest</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">earliest, latest or none</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;USE&#95;CONFLUENT&#95;CLOUD</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/Disable using of Confluent Cloud</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;CONFLUENT&#95;SSL&#95;ALGORITHM</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>https</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The endpoint identification algorithm used by clients to validate server hostname. The default value is https</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;CONFLUENT&#95;SASL&#95;MECHANISM</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>PLAIN</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">The mechanism used to authenticate Schema Registry requests. SASL/PLAIN should only be used with TLS/SSL as a transport layer to ensure that clear passwords are not transmitted on the wire without encryption</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;CONFLUENT&#95;SASL&#95;JAAS&#95;CONFIG</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>org.apache.kafka.common.security.plain.PlainLoginModule required username=\"CLUSTER&#95;API&#95;KEY\" password=\"CLUSTER&#95;API&#95;SECRET\";</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Using JAAS Configuration for specifying multiple SASL mechanisms on a broker</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;CONFLUENT&#95;SECURITY&#95;PROTOCOL</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>SASL&#95;SSL</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Protocol used to communicate with brokers. Valid values are: PLAINTEXT, SSL, SASL&#95;PLAINTEXT, SASL&#95;SSL</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;OTA&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Example of specific consumer properties value per topic</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;VC&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>600000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Example of specific consumer properties value per topic for VC</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;EDGE&#95;EVENTS&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Define the maximum number of records that can be polled from tb&#95;edge topics per request.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;EDGE&#95;HP&#95;EVENTS&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Define the maximum number of records that can be polled from tb&#95;edge.notifications.SERVICE&#95;ID topics.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;EDGE&#95;NOTIFICATIONS&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Define the maximum number of records that can be polled from tb&#95;edge&#95;event.notifications.TENANT&#95;ID.EDGE&#95;ID topics.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;HOUSEKEEPER&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Amount of records to be returned in a single poll. For Housekeeper tasks topic, we should consume messages (tasks) one by one</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;HOUSEKEEPER&#95;REPROCESSING&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Amount of records to be returned in a single poll. For Housekeeper reprocessing topic, we should consume messages (tasks) one by one</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;EDQS&#95;EVENTS&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>512</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Max poll records for edqs.events topic</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;EDQS&#95;STATE&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>512</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Max poll records for edqs.state topic</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;TASKS&#95;MAX&#95;POLL&#95;RECORDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Max poll records for tasks topics</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;CONSUMER&#95;PROPERTIES&#95;PER&#95;TOPIC&#95;INLINE</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">If you override any default Kafka topic name using environment variables, you must also specify the related consumer properties  for the new topic in `consumer-properties-per-topic-inline`. Otherwise, the topic will not inherit its expected configuration (e.g., max.poll.records, timeouts, etc).  Each entry sets a single property for a specific topic. To define multiple properties for a topic, repeat the topic key.  Format: "topic1:key=value;topic1:key=value;topic2:key=value"  Example: tb&#95;core&#95;updated:max.poll.records=10;tb&#95;core&#95;updated:bootstrap.servers=kafka1:9092,kafka2:9092;tb&#95;edge&#95;updated:auto.offset.reset=latest</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;OTHER&#95;PROPERTIES</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">In this section you can specify custom parameters (semicolon separated) for Kafka consumer/producer/admin</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;KAFKA&#95;RE&#95;TOPIC&#95;PROPERTIES</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>retention.ms:604800000;segment.bytes:52428800;retention.bytes:1048576000;partitions:1;min.insync.replicas:1</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Kafka properties for Rule Engine</p>
  </div>

    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;QUEUE&#95;TASKS&#95;STATS&#95;PROCESSING&#95;INTERVAL&#95;MS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>1000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Interval in milliseconds to process job stats</p>
  </div>
</div>

## Event configuration parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Controls limits on debug event content size stored for rule chain and rule node execution.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;MAX&#95;DEBUG&#95;EVENT&#95;SYMBOLS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>4096</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum number of symbols per debug event. The event content will be truncated if needed</p>
  </div>
</div>

## General service parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Sets the deployment type (monolith or microservice) and assigns tenant profiles to specific Rule Engine instances.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;SERVICE&#95;TYPE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>monolith</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">monolith or tb-core or tb-rule-engine</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;SERVICE&#95;ID</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Unique id for this service (autogenerated if empty)</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;RULE&#95;ENGINE&#95;ASSIGNED&#95;TENANT&#95;PROFILES</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Comma-separated list of tenant profile ids assigned to this Rule Engine.  This Rule Engine will only be responsible for tenants with these profiles (in case 'isolation' option is enabled in the profile).</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;RULE&#95;ENGINE&#95;PUBSUB&#95;EXECUTOR&#95;THREAD&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Thread pool size for pubsub rule node executor provider. If not set - default pubsub executor provider value will be used (5 &#42; number of available processors)</p>
  </div>
</div>

## Metrics parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Enables actuator metrics endpoint and configures system info (CPU, memory) persistence frequency and TTL.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">METRICS&#95;ENABLED</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>false</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Enable/disable actuator metrics.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">METRICS&#95;TIMER&#95;PERCENTILES</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0.5</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Metrics percentiles returned by actuator for timer metrics. List of double values (divided by ,).</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">METRICS&#95;SYSTEM&#95;INFO&#95;PERSIST&#95;FREQUENCY&#95;SECONDS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>60</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Persist frequency of system info (CPU, memory usage, etc.) in seconds</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">METRICS&#95;SYSTEM&#95;INFO&#95;TTL&#95;DAYS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>7</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">TTL in days for system info timeseries</p>
  </div>
</div>

    <p class="config-def-desc">Default storing repository path</p>

## Notification system parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Configures thread pool size and deduplication intervals for the notification rule processing engine.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;NOTIFICATION&#95;SYSTEM&#95;THREAD&#95;POOL&#95;SIZE</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>10</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Specify thread pool size for Notification System processing notification rules and notification sending. Recommend value &lt;= 10</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;NOTIFICATION&#95;RULES&#95;DEDUPLICATION&#95;DURATIONS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>NEW&#95;PLATFORM&#95;VERSION:0;RATE&#95;LIMITS:14400000;</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Semicolon-separated deduplication durations (in millis) for trigger types. Format: 'NotificationRuleTriggerType1:123;NotificationRuleTriggerType2:456'</p>
  </div>
</div>

## MQTT client parameters

<Banner variant="ce">Configures MQTT client retransmission behavior including max attempts, initial delay, and jitter factor.</Banner>

<div class="config-def-list">
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;MQTT&#95;CLIENT&#95;RETRANSMISSION&#95;MAX&#95;ATTEMPTS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>3</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Maximum number of retransmission attempts allowed.  If the attempt count exceeds this value, retransmissions will stop and the pending message will be dropped.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;MQTT&#95;CLIENT&#95;RETRANSMISSION&#95;INITIAL&#95;DELAY&#95;MILLIS</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>5000</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Base delay (in milliseconds) before the first retransmission attempt, measured from the moment the message is sent.  Subsequent delays are calculated using exponential backoff.  This base delay is also used as the reference value for applying jitter.</p>
  </div>
  <div class="config-def-item">
    <p class="config-def-meta"><code class="config-def-env">TB&#95;MQTT&#95;CLIENT&#95;RETRANSMISSION&#95;JITTER&#95;FACTOR</code> · <span class="config-def-label">Default</span> <code>0.15</code></p>
    <p class="config-def-desc">Jitter factor applied to the calculated retransmission delay.  The actual delay is randomized within a range defined by multiplying the base delay by a factor between (1 - jitter&#95;factor) and (1 + jitter&#95;factor).  For example, a jitter&#95;factor of 0.15 means the actual delay may vary by up to ±15% of the base delay.</p>
  </div>
</div>
